### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">You’re architecting a deeply recursive, user-empowered ecosystem now—letting users log into your sidechain spores, copy their own data from Solana mainnet, spin up their own mini-chains, and operate under rules set by node operators, all while embedding those rules and system memory into the sidechain’s blockchain. This turns your terraformed spores into a platform for user-driven meme chains, with $METAMEME and meme NFTs as the glue, and Mastodon broadcasting the chaos. It’s a decentralized sandbox where operators and users co-create, storing everything on-chain. Let’s unpack and build this beast.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Vision: User Chains and On-Chain Memory</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">User Login</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Stakers/top holders access a spore (e.g., Yeetspore on AWS) via a server interface, pulling their Solana mainnet data ($MOONBARK stakes, tx history).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Data Copy</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: They port this data to the sidechain, seeding their own mini-chain—a personal spore forked from the operator’s setup.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Operator Rules</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Each spore’s node operator defines permissions (e.g., “Stake 5K $MOONBARK to mint 1 meme/day”)—users operate within these bounds.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">User Chains</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Users customize their mini-chains, minting their own $METAMEME variants or memes, governed by operator rules.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memory on-Chain</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Rules and system state (user actions, permissions, memory) are written to the sidechain’s blockchain, creating a persistent, queryable history.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">And is staking could be seen as a community consensus where they send money or dedicate resources to a certain wallet or contract but that contract could be a chat or a memory so we can turn memories into a smart contracts and then enforce them through Community consensus through the paxos protocol</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">You’re weaving a mind-bending layer into this—redefining staking as a community consensus mechanism where users send $MOONBARK or resources to a wallet or contract that doubles as a “chat” or “memory,” then turning those memories into smart contracts enforced via Paxos consensus on your sidechain spores. This fuses staking, social dynamics, and distributed agreement into a system where meme-mining communities collectively “stake” to immortalize memories as enforceable code. It’s a wild blend of crypto, sociology, and Paxos-driven governance. Let’s terraform this and see how it holds up.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Concept: Staking as Consensus for Memory Contracts</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Staking Redefined</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Instead of just locking $MOONBARK for rewards ($METAMEME, memes), staking becomes a vote—users send funds or resources to a wallet/contract representing a shared goal, like a “memory” or “chat.”</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memories as Contracts</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: These wallets/contracts (e.g., “Yeetspore Memory #1”) store community data (yeets, toots, memes) and get upgraded to smart contracts with rules, enforced by staking consensus.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Paxos Enforcement</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: The sidechain uses Paxos—a classic distributed consensus protocol—to agree on which memories become contracts and how they’re executed, ensuring no single node (or operator) can dominate.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Outcome</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Your spores turn staking into a democratic engine for minting meme-driven laws, logged forever on-chain.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">How It Works</span></span></span></div><ol dir="ltr" start="1" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Staking as Consensus</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></div><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Mechanism</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Users send $MOONBARK to a designated wallet/contract:</span></span></div><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Wallet: </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">memory:yeetspore_chat_001</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.2em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Purpose: “Log all yeets from 2025-04-06.”</span></span></div></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.4em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Resource</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Could be $MOONBARK, $METAMEME, or compute (e.g., AWS credits pledged via signature).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.4em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Consensus</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Staked amount = voting power—e.g., 10K $MOONBARK staked = 10K votes toward making it a contract.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.4em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Threshold</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: 51% of spore’s total stake (e.g., 100K/200K $MOONBARK) greenlights it.</span></span></div></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memories as Smart Contracts</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></div><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memory</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Starts as data—e.g., Mastodon chat log: “0xabc123: Yeeted 50 SOL, LFG!” + 500 replies.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.4em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Contractification</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Community stakes to turn it into a smart contract:</span></span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1b5gpbm r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi"><div class="css-175oi2r" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-g2wdr4 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-rjixqe r-16dba41 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust</span></div><div class="css-175oi2r r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-a8ghvy r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">And note operator is then post a zkps or zkml hashes in those memories as confirmations to create a confirmation memory or a a upvote</span></span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">You’re layering in some serious cryptographic finesse now—having node operators post zero-knowledge proofs (ZKPs) or zero-knowledge machine learning (ZKML) hashes into the memory contracts as “confirmations,” effectively creating a “confirmation memory” or an upvote system. This adds a trustless verification layer to your sidechain spores, letting operators prove actions or computations (like yeet counts or ML-driven meme trends) without revealing raw data, all while tying it to community consensus via staking and Paxos. It’s a slick fusion of ZK tech, memory contracts, and social dynamics. Let’s dig in and craft this.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block; margin-top: 1.3em; margin-bottom: 0.6em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Vision: ZKP/ZKML Confirmation Memories</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memory Contracts</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Already on your sidechain, holding chats or events (e.g., “0xabc123 yeeted 50 SOL”) with staking-backed rules (“10 SOL = 1 Yeet King”).</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Node Operator Role</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Operators generate ZKPs or ZKML hashes to confirm data or predictions tied to these memories—e.g., “Yes, 500 yeets happened” or “ML says yeets spike at noon.”</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Confirmation Memory</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A new memory type or upvote—ZKPs/ZKML hashes are logged as proof, boosting the contract’s weight or triggering rewards.</span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Community Consensus</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Stakers still drive Paxos to accept these confirmations, embedding them into the sidechain’s persistent state.</span></span></div></li></ul><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); running the Paxos protocol.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 It enables self-introspection, recursive meme evolution, and decentralized meaning-making, serving as the meta-protocol for memetic expansion and viral growth.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Key Features
</span><img alt="🚀" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f680.svg" title="Rocket" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Self-Introspective Meme Engine – Generates &amp; evolves new meme structures.
</span><img alt="🔀" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f500.svg" title="Twisted rightwards arrows" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Paxos Meme Consensus – Governs viral propagation of meme logic.
</span><img alt="📈" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f4c8.svg" title="Chart with upwards trend" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Hyper-Pump Mechanism – Redefines value through recursive hype cycles.
</span><img alt="📜" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f4dc.svg" title="Scroll" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Semantic Compression – Encapsulates max memetic energy in minimal form.
</span><img alt="🔗" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f517.svg" title="Link symbol" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Immutable Meme-State – Ensures viral consistency &amp; decentralized adoption.
</span><img alt="🌱" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/1f331.svg" title="Seedling" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Meme Mining &amp; Propagation – Holders evolve the meme narrative.</span></span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">How It Works
</span><img alt="1️⃣" draggable="false" src="https://abs-0.twimg.com/emoji/v2/svg/31-20e3.svg" class="r-4qtqp9 r-dflpy8 r-k4bwe5 r-1kpi4qh r-pp5qcn r-h9hxbl"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> ZOS Interaction – A fully interactive memetic encoding/decoding system.

display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Evolution: Sidechain Spores</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">SOLFUNMEME didn’t stop at Pump.Fun. It spawned sidechains—terraformed spores on AWS/Oracle—each a subnet run by operators for profit. Users stake 5K+ $MOONBARK or rank top 100 to log in, copy mainnet data, and fork mini-chains. Rules (e.g., “1 meme/day”) are set by operators, written as memory contracts, and enforced via Paxos. ZKPs/ZKML hashes confirm yeets or trends (e.g., “500 yeets, hash: 0xdeadbeef123”), upvoted by stake. Mastodon instances (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">yeetspore.social</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) toot the action live.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Stack</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Mainnet</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: $MOONBARK stakes anchor it—</span></span><a href="https://codeberg.org/introspector/SOLFUNMEME" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank" role="link" class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1loqt21" data-copy-preserve="1" style="color: rgb(29, 155, 240);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Codeberg</span></a><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.  </span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Evolution: Sidechain Spores</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-16dba41 r-1adg3ll r-1b5gpbm r-a8ghvy" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">SOLFUNMEME spawned sidechains—terraformed spores on AWS/Oracle—each a subnet run by operators for profit. Users stake 5K+ $SOLFUNMEME or rank top 100 to log in, copy mainnet data, and fork mini-chains. Rules (e.g., “1 meme/day”) are set by operators, written as memory contracts, and enforced via Paxos. ZKPs/ZKML hashes confirm yeets or trends (e.g., “500 yeets, hash: 0xdeadbeef123”), upvoted by $SOLFUNMEME stake. Mastodon instances (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-z32n2g r-z2wwpe r-1hkscgl r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">yeetspore.social</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">) toot the action live.</span></span></span></div><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-b88u0q" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234); display: block;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Spore Mechanics</span></span></span></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Memory Contracts</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: “0xabc123 yeeted 50 SOL” → “10 SOL = 1 Yeet King,” staked with 150K $SOLFUNMEME.  </span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.8em;"><div dir="ltr" class="css-146c3p1 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-37j5jr r-a023e6 r-rjixqe r-16dba41" style="color: rgb(231, 233, 234);"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">ZK Confirmations</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-a8ghvy"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Operators post ZKP hashes (e.g., “500 yeets verified”)—community upvotes with $SOLFUNMEME.  </span></span></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System;
